You said:

looking to buy a fun party game, what should we get?

ChatGPT said:

If you want a party game that actually lands, the big things to look for are easy rules, quick rounds, and high interaction (so people aren’t sitting bored). The best ones usually lean into humour, bluffing, or chaos rather than strategy Wargamer.
